<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#e33d3d>Sotoru, Daigen Daigen received the message about the urgent need to repair the southern bridge, destroyed in the recent attack. Understanding the importance of this task for the village, he immediately headed towards the damaged area, determined to contribute in any way he could.

Upon arriving at the bridge, Daigen saw many villagers already hard at work. The sight of everyone coming together filled him with a sense of purpose. He quickly found a section where his help was needed. Lifting heavy wooden beams and carrying them to the construction site, Daigen worked alongside others, his physical training paying off as he managed the strenuous tasks with relative ease.

As the day progressed, Daigen's hands became calloused, and his muscles ached from the constant lifting and hammering. Despite the physical toll, he continued without complaint, motivated by the knowledge that his efforts would help restore a critical part of the village's infrastructure. The camaraderie among the villagers, their shared determination, and the occasional encouraging words from one another fueled his resolve to see the task through to completion.

By the end of the day, significant progress had been made on the bridge. Daigen stood back for a moment, wiping the sweat from his brow, and surveyed the work done. The bridge was not yet fully repaired, but the combined efforts of the villagers had brought it much closer to being operational again. Feeling a deep sense of accomplishment and community, Daigen knew that his contribution had made a difference.</font></font></font>
